Cleanup

Cleanup#

This notebook just cleans up the images folder to make it small enough to upload it to github.

import pandas as pd
from pathlib import Path

# Paths
csv_file = "data.csv"
images_dir = Path("images")

# Read valid paths from CSV
df = pd.read_csv(csv_file)

# Normalize paths for cross-platform compatibility
valid_paths = {
    Path(p).as_posix()
    for p in df["filename"].astype(str)
}

# Recursively scan all files in images/
for file_path in images_dir.rglob("*"):
    if not file_path.is_file():
        continue

    # Path relative to images/
    relative_path = file_path.relative_to(images_dir).as_posix()

    if relative_path not in valid_paths:
        print(f"Deleting: {file_path}")
        file_path.unlink()

print("Done.")
